          <div data-target="readme-toc.content" class="Box-body px-5 pb-5">
            <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><h1 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-norad-two-line-element-set-norad-tle" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#norad-two-line-element-set-norad-tle"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>NORAD Two-line element set (NORAD TLE)</h1>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-orbitalcpp-implementation-in-c-was-written-by-kingsley-otengamoako--2019-2020" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#orbitalcpp-implementation-in-c-was-written-by-kingsley-otengamoako--2019-2020"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>orbital.cpp implementation in C++ was written by Kingsley OtengAmoako © 2019, 2020.</h3>
<p dir="auto">Two-line element set (TLE) data format parser.</p>
<p dir="auto">The US Air Force provides data for Earth-orbiting satellites in Two-Line Orbital Element Sets (<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Two-line_element_set" rel="nofollow">TLE</a>). The current TLE format is specified by <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/NORAD" rel="nofollow">NORAD</a> with input from <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/NASA" rel="nofollow">NASA</a>.  A derivation of the Two-Line Element set format called the Three-Line Element set exists where the first line contains the name of the satellite. These element sets are general perturbation mean elements constructed by a least squares estimation from observations. The Air Force provides the observations taken from the Space Surveillance Network, and FreeFlyer provides the capability of simulating observations to generate TLEs. The TLE elements may be propogated using an <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SGP4" rel="nofollow">SGP4</a> model (or one of the SGP8, <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SDP4" rel="nofollow">SDP4</a>, SDP8 models).</p>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-format" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#format"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Format</h2>
<p dir="auto"><strong>More,  detailed information is available at <a href="http://spaceflight.nasa.gov/realdata/sightings/SSapplications/Post/JavaSSOP/SSOP_Help/tle_def.html" rel="nofollow">NASA Human Space Flight</a>:</strong></p>
<h3 align="center" tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content---------" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#--------"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>
  <a href="http://spaceflight.nasa.gov/realdata/sightings/SSapplications/Post/JavaSSOP/SSOP_Help/tle_def.html" rel="nofollow">
    <img alt="Definition of Two-line Element Set Coordinate System" src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/97e912668ab83b86bca13347c515d4ddeb3cfc73d4be558ef27d37b74b04b77e/687474703a2f2f7370616365666c696768742e6e6173612e676f762f7265616c646174612f7369676874696e67732f53536170706c69636174696f6e732f506f73742f4a61766153534f502f53534f505f48656c702f326c696e652e676966" data-animated-image="" data-canonical-src="http://spaceflight.nasa.gov/realdata/sightings/SSapplications/Post/JavaSSOP/SSOP_Help/2line.gif" style="max-width: 100%;">
  </a>
</h3>
<p dir="auto">Some data to play around with can be found at <a href="http://www.celestrak.com/NORAD/elements/" rel="nofollow">Celestrak</a> and in <a href="http://www.celestrak.com/NORAD/elements/master.asp" rel="nofollow">Celestrak's Master Index</a>.</p>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-usage-from-url" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#usage-from-url"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Usage from URL</h2>

<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-parsing-a-single-set" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#parsing-a-single-set"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Parsing a single set</h3>

<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-creating-a-tle-instance-from-existing-data" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#creating-a-tle-instance-from-existing-data"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Creating a TLE instance from existing data</h2>
